Basic Elements","","### Headings","","Different levels of headings for structuring content.","","# Heading 1","","The largest heading, usually reserved for the main title of the document. By default, single `#` in markdown is converted to Title. Thus, 'Heading 2', which in markdown is `## Heading 2` will have Heading 1 style applied, unless you set `useTitle` to false in the `sectionProps`.","","## Heading 2","","A subheading, used to separate major sections.","","### Heading 3","","A smaller heading, often used for subsections.","","#### Heading 4","","A more detailed subsection heading.","","##### Heading 5","","A minor heading, used for further breakdown.","","###### Heading 6","","The smallest heading, typically used for fine details.","","\u003e #### Nested Blockquote Example","\u003e","\u003e \u003e ##### Nested Blockquote Level 2","\u003e \u003e","\u003e \u003e - List inside a blockquote:","\u003e \u003e   - **Bold Text** inside a list","\u003e \u003e   - `Inline Code` inside a list","\u003e \u003e","\u003e \u003e ```javascript","\u003e \u003e console.log(\"Code inside a blockquote list\");","\u003e \u003e ```","","### Text Formatting","","- **Bold text `with code`**","- _Italic text_","- ~~Strikethrough~~","- `Inline code`","","### Blockquote","","\u003e This is a **nested blockquote** example.","\u003e","\u003e \u003e Another level of nesting.","\u003e \u003e","\u003e \u003e - List item 1","\u003e \u003e - List item 2","\u003e \u003e   - Subitem inside blockquote","\u003e \u003e","\u003e \u003e ```python","\u003e \u003e def nested_function():","\u003e \u003e     return \"Code inside nested blockquote\"","\u003e \u003e ```","","### Horizontal Rule","","---","","## 2. Math Equations (KaTeX / LaTeX)","","Displaying mathematical expressions.","","Inline equation: $E=mc^2$","","Block equation:","","$$","\\sum_{n=1}^{\\infty} \\frac{1}{n^2} = \\frac{\\pi^2}{6}","$$","","### Inline Math","","Inline math expressions can be enclosed within single dollar signs: $E=mc^2$. You can also use `\\\\(` and `\\\\)`: $\\sum_{i=1}^{n} i^2$. With hat \"$$\\hat{x}$$\".","","### Display Math","","Display math expressions are enclosed within double dollar signs, which renders them on their own line:","","$$","\\int_0^\\infty x^2 e^{-x^2} dx = \\frac{\\sqrt{\\pi}}{4}","$$","","You can also use `\\\\[` and `\\\\]`:","","$$","\\frac{d}{dx} \\left( \\frac{1}{x} \\right) = -\\frac{1}{x^2}","$$","","### Common Math Symbols","","Here are some common mathematical symbols:","","- Greek letters: $\\alpha$, $\\beta$, $\\gamma$, $\\Gamma$, $\\Delta$, $\\pi$, $\\Pi$, $\\Sigma$, $\\omega$, $\\Omega$","- Superscripts and subscripts: $x^2$, $y_i$, $a^{b+c}$, $e^{-i\\omega t}$","- Fractions: $\\frac{1}{2}$, $\\frac{x+y}{z}$","- Square roots: $\\sqrt{x}$, $\\sqrt[3]{y}$","- Summations and products: $\\sum_{i=1}^n i$, $\\prod_{j=1}^m j$","- Integrals: $\\int_a^b f(x) dx$, $\\oint_C \\vec{F} \\cdot d\\vec{r}$","- Limits: $\\lim_{x \\to \\infty} \\frac{1}{x}$","- Vectors: $\\vec{v}$, $\\mathbf{v}$","- Matrices: $\\begin{pmatrix} a \u0026 b \\\\ c \u0026 d \\end{pmatrix}$","- Partial derivatives: $\\frac{\\partial f}{\\partial x}$","- Infinity: $\\infty$","- Logical symbols: $\\forall$, $\\exists$, $\\in$, $\\notin$, $\\subseteq$, $\\supseteq$, $\\land$, $\\lor$, $\\neg$","- Trigonometric functions: $\\sin(x)$, $\\cos(y)$, $\\tan(z)$","- Exponential and logarithmic functions: $e^x$, $\\ln(y)$, $\\log_{10}(z)$","","### Matrices","","Matrices can be created using the `pmatrix`, `bmatrix`, `vmatrix`, and `Vmatrix` environments:","","$$","\\begin{pmatrix}","1 \u0026 2 \u0026 3 \\\\","4 \u0026 5 \u0026 6 \\\\","7 \u0026 8 \u0026 9","\\end{pmatrix}","$$","","$$","\\begin{bmatrix}","1 \u0026 2 \\\\","3 \u0026 4","\\end{bmatrix}","$$","","$$","\\begin{vmatrix}","a \u0026 b \\\\","c \u0026 d","\\end{vmatrix}","$$","","$$","\\begin{Vmatrix}","a \u0026 b \\\\","c \u0026 d","\\end{Vmatrix}","$$","","### Alignments","","You can align equations using the `align` environment:","","$$","\\begin{align}","y \u0026= mx + b \\\\","y' \u0026= m","\\end{align}","$$","","You can also use `aligned` for aligning parts of an equation:","","$$","f(x) = \\begin{cases}","x^2, \u0026 \\text{if } x \\ge 0 \\\\","-x^2, \u0026 \\text{otherwise}","\\end{cases}","$$","","$$","\\begin{aligned}","(a+b)^2 \u0026= (a+b)(a+b) \\\\","\u0026= a^2 + ab + ba + b^2 \\\\","\u0026= a^2 + 2ab + b^2","\\end{aligned}","$$","","### Case Statements","","Case statements can be created using the `cases` environment:","","$$","f(x) =","\\begin{cases}","1, \u0026 \\text{if } x \u003e 0 \\\\","0, \u0026 \\text{if } x = 0 \\\\","-1, \u0026 \\text{if } x \u003c 0","\\end{cases}","$$","","### Text in Math","","You can include text within math expressions using the `\\text{}` command:","","$$","\\text{Let } x \\text{ be a real number.}","$$","","### Colored Math","","You can color math expressions using the `\\textcolor{color}{math}` command:","","$$","\\textcolor{red}{E=mc^2}","$$","","$$","\\textcolor{blue}{\\sum_{i=1}^n i}","$$","","### Math Macros","","You can define custom macros:","","```latex","\\newcommand{\\norm}[1]{\\left\\lVert#1\\right\\rVert}","```","","## 10. <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1. Basic Elements</h2><a id="user-content-1-basic-elements" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1. Basic Elements" href="#1-basic-elements"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Headings</h3><a id="user-content-headings" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Headings" href="#headings"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Different levels of headings for structuring content.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Heading 1</h1><a id="user-content-heading-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Heading 1" href="#heading-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The largest heading, usually reserved for the main title of the document. By default, single <code>#</code> in markdown is converted to Title. Thus, 'Heading 2', which in markdown is <code>## Heading 2</code> will have Heading 1 style applied, unless you set <code>useTitle</code> to false in the <code>sectionProps</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Heading 2</h2><a id="user-content-heading-2" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Heading 2" href="#heading-2"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A subheading, used to separate major sections.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Heading 3</h3><a id="user-content-heading-3" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Heading 3" href="#heading-3"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A smaller heading, often used for subsections.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Heading 4</h4><a id="user-content-heading-4" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Heading 4" href="#heading-4"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A more detailed subsection heading.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Heading 5</h5><a id="user-content-heading-5" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Heading 5" href="#heading-5"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A minor heading, used for further breakdown.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h6 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Heading 6</h6><a id="user-content-heading-6" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Heading 6" href="#heading-6"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The smallest heading, typically used for fine details.</p>
<blockquote>

</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="console.log(&quot;Code inside a blockquote list&quot;);"><pre><span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"Code inside a blockquote list"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</blockquote>
</blockquote>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Text Formatting</h3><a id="user-content-text-formatting" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Text Formatting" href="#text-formatting"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Bold text <code>with code</code></strong></li>
<li><em>Italic text</em></li>
<li><del>Strikethrough</del></li>
<li><code>Inline code</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Blockquote</h3><a id="user-content-blockquote" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Blockquote" href="#blockquote"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<blockquote>

</li>
</ul>

    return &quot;Code inside nested blockquote&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">nested_function</span>():

<p dir="auto">You can define a reference link like this<br>
<a href="https://openai.com" title="OpenAI Website" rel="nofollow">OpenAI</a> is an AI research and deployment company.</p>
<p dir="auto">Markdown syntax is explained in detail on <a href="https://www.markdownguide.org" title="Markdown Guide" rel="nofollow">Markdown Guide</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">References</h4><a id="user-content-references" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: References" href="#references"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">6. Task Lists (GFM)</h2><a id="user-content-6-task-lists-gfm" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 6. <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">7. Footnotes</h2><a id="user-content-7-footnotes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 7. <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">8. Emoji (GFM)</h2><a id="user-content-8-emoji-gfm" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 8. <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">9. Math Equations (KaTeX / LaTeX)</h2><a id="user-content-9-math-equations-katex--latex" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 9. Math Equations (KaTeX / LaTeX)" href="#9-math-equations-katex--latex"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Displaying mathematical expressions.</p>
<p dir="auto">Inline equation: <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$E=mc^2$</math-renderer></p>
<p dir="auto">Block equation:</p>
<p dir="auto"><math-renderer class="js-display-math" style="display: block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$$
\sum_{n=1}^{\infty} \frac{1}{n^2} = \frac{\pi^2}{6}
$$</math-renderer></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Inline Math</h3><a id="user-content-inline-math" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Inline Math" href="#inline-math"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Inline math expressions can be enclosed within single dollar signs: <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$E=mc^2$</math-renderer>. You can also use <code>\\(</code> and <code>\\)</code>: <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\sum_{i=1}^{n} i^2$</math-renderer>. With hat "$$\hat{x}$$".</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Display Math</h3><a id="user-content-display-math" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Display Math" href="#display-math"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Display math expressions are enclosed within double dollar signs, which renders them on their own line:</p>
<p dir="auto"><math-renderer class="js-display-math" style="display: block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$$
\int_0^\infty x^2 e^{-x^2} dx = \frac{\sqrt{\pi}}{4}
$$</math-renderer></p>
<p dir="auto">You can also use <code>\\[</code> and <code>\\]</code>:</p>
<p dir="auto"><math-renderer class="js-display-math" style="display: block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$$
\frac{d}{dx} \left( \frac{1}{x} \right) = -\frac{1}{x^2}
$$</math-renderer></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Common Math Symbols</h3><a id="user-content-common-math-symbols" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Common Math Symbols" href="#common-math-symbols"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Here are some common mathematical symbols:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Greek letters: <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\alpha$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\beta$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\gamma$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\Gamma$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\Delta$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\pi$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\Pi$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\Sigma$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\omega$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\Omega$</math-renderer>
</li>
<li>Superscripts and subscripts: <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$x^2$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$y_i$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$a^{b+c}$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$e^{-i\omega t}$</math-renderer>
</li>
<li>Fractions: <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\frac{1}{2}$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\frac{x+y}{z}$</math-renderer>
</li>
<li>Square roots: <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\sqrt{x}$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\sqrt[3]{y}$</math-renderer>
</li>
<li>Summations and products: <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\sum_{i=1}^n i$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\prod_{j=1}^m j$</math-renderer>
</li>
<li>Integrals: <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\int_a^b f(x) dx$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\oint_C \vec{F} \cdot d\vec{r}$</math-renderer>
</li>
<li>Limits: <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\lim_{x \to \infty} \frac{1}{x}$</math-renderer>
</li>
<li>Vectors: <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\vec{v}$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\mathbf{v}$</math-renderer>
</li>
<li>Matrices: $\begin{pmatrix} a &amp; b \ c &amp; d \end{pmatrix}$</li>
<li>Partial derivatives: <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\frac{\partial f}{\partial x}$</math-renderer>
</li>
<li>Infinity: <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\infty$</math-renderer>
</li>
<li>Logical symbols: <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\forall$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\exists$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\in$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\notin$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\subseteq$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\supseteq$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\land$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\lor$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\neg$</math-renderer>
</li>
<li>Trigonometric functions: <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\sin(x)$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\cos(y)$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\tan(z)$</math-renderer>
</li>
<li>Exponential and logarithmic functions: <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$e^x$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\ln(y)$</math-renderer>, <math-renderer class="js-inline-math" style="display: inline-block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$\log_{10}(z)$</math-renderer>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Matrices</h3><a id="user-content-matrices" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Matrices" href="#matrices"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Matrices can be created using the <code>pmatrix</code>, <code>bmatrix</code>, <code>vmatrix</code>, and <code>Vmatrix</code> environments:</p>
<p dir="auto"><math-renderer class="js-display-math" style="display: block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$$
\begin{pmatrix}
1 &amp; 2 &amp; 3 \\
4 &amp; 5 &amp; 6 \\
7 &amp; 8 &amp; 9
\end{pmatrix}
$$</math-renderer></p>
<p dir="auto"><math-renderer class="js-display-math" style="display: block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$$
\begin{bmatrix}
1 &amp; 2 \\
3 &amp; 4
\end{bmatrix}
$$</math-renderer></p>
<p dir="auto"><math-renderer class="js-display-math" style="display: block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$$
\begin{vmatrix}
a &amp; b \\
c &amp; d
\end{vmatrix}
$$</math-renderer></p>
<p dir="auto"><math-renderer class="js-display-math" style="display: block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$$
\begin{Vmatrix}
a &amp; b \\
c &amp; d
\end{Vmatrix}
$$</math-renderer></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Alignments</h3><a id="user-content-alignments" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Alignments" href="#alignments"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You can align equations using the <code>align</code> environment:</p>
<p dir="auto"><math-renderer class="js-display-math" style="display: block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$$
\begin{align}
y &amp;= mx + b \\
y' &amp;= m
\end{align}
$$</math-renderer></p>
<p dir="auto">You can also use <code>aligned</code> for aligning parts of an equation:</p>
<p dir="auto"><math-renderer class="js-display-math" style="display: block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$$
f(x) = \begin{cases}
x^2, &amp; \text{if } x \ge 0 \\
-x^2, &amp; \text{otherwise}
\end{cases}
$$</math-renderer></p>
<p dir="auto"><math-renderer class="js-display-math" style="display: block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$$
\begin{aligned}
(a+b)^2 &amp;= (a+b)(a+b) \\
&amp;= a^2 + ab + ba + b^2 \\
&amp;= a^2 + 2ab + b^2
\end{aligned}
$$</math-renderer></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Case Statements</h3><a id="user-content-case-statements" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Case Statements" href="#case-statements"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Case statements can be created using the <code>cases</code> environment:</p>
<p dir="auto"><math-renderer class="js-display-math" style="display: block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$$
f(x) =
\begin{cases}
1, &amp; \text{if } x &gt; 0 \\
0, &amp; \text{if } x = 0 \\
-1, &amp; \text{if } x &lt; 0
\end{cases}
$$</math-renderer></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Text in Math</h3><a id="user-content-text-in-math" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Text in Math" href="#text-in-math"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You can include text within math expressions using the <code>\text{}</code> command:</p>
<p dir="auto"><math-renderer class="js-display-math" style="display: block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$$
\text{Let } x \text{ be a real number.}
$$</math-renderer></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Colored Math</h3><a id="user-content-colored-math" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Colored Math" href="#colored-math"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You can color math expressions using the <code>\textcolor{color}{math}</code> command:</p>
<p dir="auto"><math-renderer class="js-display-math" style="display: block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$$
\textcolor{red}{E=mc^2}
$$</math-renderer></p>
<p dir="auto"><math-renderer class="js-display-math" style="display: block" data-run-id="687fe06ad252903d644af453c44942f6">$$
\textcolor{blue}{\sum_{i=1}^n i}
$$</math-renderer></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Math Macros</h3><a id="user-content-math-macros" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Math Macros" href="#math-macros"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You can define custom macros:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-tex-latex notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="\newcommand{\norm}[1]{\left\lVert#1\right\rVert}"><pre><span class="pl-k">\newcommand</span>{<span class="pl-c1">\norm</span>}[1]{<span class="pl-c1">\left\lVert</span>#1<span class="pl-c1">\right\rVert</span>}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">10. Diagrams (Mermaid)</h2><a id="user-content-10-diagrams-mermaid" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 10. Diagrams (Mermaid)" href="#10-diagrams-mermaid"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Visualizing data with diagrams.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Flowchart</h3><a id="user-content-flowchart" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Flowchart" href="#flowchart"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Sequence Diagram</h3><a id="user-content-sequence-diagram" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Sequence Diagram" href="#sequence-diagram"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
